## Why adam

adam is a **deterministic cognitive kernel for Kazakh** вАФ rule-based dialog with auditable belief revision, morpheme-indexed retrieval, and a forward-chaining reasoner over typed facts, all running as a single tool-driven pipeline. It trades **generalisation for integrity**: every output is traceable, every belief revisable, every conclusion sourced. Every layer is **Rust-only** and **graph-first** by repository invariant вАФ both enforced by contract tests.

### Engineering thesis

The project's core engineering claim вАФ independent of any historical or philosophical thesis about Kazakh вАФ is that **agglutinative morphology gives a clean algebra of meaning**: every Kazakh word decomposes into a root plus a sequence of typed suffixes, each contributing a known grammatical operator (case, number, tense, person, possessive, polarity, modality). Composition is rule-bound, not learned. That structure is exactly what we build the runtime on: FST morphology + typed suffix priors + root-pair PMI as deterministic prior layers, world_core as a curated graph of typed facts, and templates as the only path from fact to text. No probabilistic free generation. No retrained-from-scratch behaviour per release. The result is **predictable, traceable, low-energy** answer for Kazakh queries вАФ not because the language has special metaphysical status, but because its structure is unusually friendly to formal modelling. The same engineering style would apply to other agglutinative-typology languages (Turkish, Kyrgyz, Tatar, Uzbek, вА¶) without claims of universal grammar.

**v4.36.6 вАФ FST coverage: ¬Ђ–∞–ї–∞–Љ¬ї short-form 1sg + ¬Ђ–Њ“Ы–Є¬ї back-vowel converb (final v4.36.x FST gaps closed).** Patch in v4.36+ semantic-IR arc. Closes the two FST coverage gaps re-scoped from v4.36.5 to v4.36.6+. **(1)** ¬Ђ–Њ“Ы–Є¬ї back-vowel converb вАФ vowel-final back-vowel verbs change shape during converb derivation (–Њ“Ы—Л вЖТ –Њ“Ы–Є), breaking prefix-match in `surface_could_contain_root`. Pre-fix, surfaces beginning with ¬Ђ–Њ“Ы–Є*¬ї / ¬Ђ–ґ–∞—Б—Л*¬ї / ¬Ђ—В–∞–љ—Л*¬ї couldn't be analysed. **(2)** ¬Ђ–∞–ї–∞–Љ¬ї short-form 1sg вАФ colloquial Kazakh 1sg present-style verbs drop the `-—Л–љ/-—Ц–љ` tail of personal ending (-–Љ—Л–љ/-–Љ—Ц–љ вЖТ -–Љ). Synth produced only long form, so user-typed ¬Ђ–∞–ї–∞–Љ / –±–∞—А–∞–Љ / –Њ“Ы–Є–Љ¬ї didn't parse. **Implementation:** **(1)** `surface_could_contain_root` extended with —Л/—Ц вЖТ –Є vowel alternation (mirrors existing intervocalic-voicing branch). Synth side already produces ¬Ђ–Њ“Ы–Є¬ї via `apply_aorist_after_vowel`; gap was purely parser-prefix-match. **(2)** Short-form 1sg synth path inside `try_verb_analyses` nested loop вАФ when feature combo is (Present|PastEvidential) + First + (Sg|None) + polite=false, also try short-form variant by stripping trailing `-—Л–љ/-—Ц–љ` from long-form synth. Limited to 1sg (other persons don't contract in standard Kazakh). **Live verification:** ¬Ђ–Ю“Ы–Є¬ї / ¬Ђ–Ю“Ы–Є–і—Л¬ї now parse (was: no parse); ¬Ђ–Р–ї–∞–Љ¬ї / ¬Ђ–С–∞—А–∞–Љ¬ї now parse with `tense=Present person=First`; ¬Ђ–Ц–∞–Ј–∞ –∞–ї–∞–Љ¬ї вЖТ "–Ц–∞“Ы—Б—Л –µ–Ї–µ–љ, —Б—Ц–Ј–і—Ц“£ –Љ“ѓ–Љ–Ї—Ц–љ–і—Ц–≥—Ц“£—Ц–Ј–і—Ц —В“ѓ—Б—Ц–љ–і—Ц–Љ." (full ability detection works on short form); long forms ¬Ђ–∞–ї–∞–Љ—Л–љ¬ї unchanged. **Verification:** Workspace **865 passing** unchanged; real-world **26-query battery 26/26 = 100 % coherent**; mean **216.1 ms / 177.1 MB** (+21 ms vs v4.36.5 вАФ real perf cost from vowel-alternation check + short-form synth+compare per matching feature combo; honest trade for closing two architectural gaps); facts 1934 unchanged; all holdouts unchanged; foundation passes. **v4.36.x arc complete** вАФ three releases (v4.36.0 вЖТ v4.36.5 вЖТ v4.36.6) closed all v4.36+ FST coverage and consumption work. Hearsay-detection chain now end-to-end functional on natural Kazakh forms across all relevant tense/person variants. Pipeline: 1 extension to `surface_could_contain_root` (~10 lines) + 1 new conditional in `try_verb_analyses` short-form path (~20 lines) + facts version sync. Cadence: patch вАФ two FST gaps closed; honest +21 ms perf cost. **Stripe (9) вАФ semantic IR layer continues.** Next: v4.36.7 (Evidence on extraction side); v4.37.0 (fourth matcher migration; remaining 6 parser tenses; ¬ЂX –µ–Љ–µ—Б –њ–µ?¬ї question form).

**v4.36.5 вАФ FST coverage: ConverbPerfect + PastReportative (¬Ђ–ґ–∞–Ј—Л–њ—В—Л¬ї / ¬Ђ–±–Њ–ї—Л–њ—В—Л¬ї now route to Hearsay).** Patch in v4.36+ semantic-IR arc. Closes the v4.36.0 honest-gap carry-forward вАФ the ¬Ђ-{Y}–њ(—В—Л)¬ї reportative form, which is the natural Kazakh hearsay form most commonly produced in user dialog, previously didn't parse at all. **Before:** ¬Ђ–Ц–∞–Ј—Л–њ—В—Л¬ї вЖТ "–Ґ“ѓ—Б—Ц–љ–±–µ–і—Ц–Љ." **After:** "–°—Ц–Ј–≥–µ –∞–є—В—Л–ї“У–∞–љ —Б–Є—П“Ы—В—Л –µ–Ї–µ–љ вАФ –љ–∞“Ы—В—Л –і–µ—А–µ–≥—Ц–Љ –ґ–Њ“Ы." **(1)** New `Tense::PastReportative` variant, distinct from `PastEvidential` (both encode hearsay but differ structurally: PastEvidential = `-“У–∞–љ/-–≥–µ–љ` participle base + person endings; PastReportative = `-{Y}–њ` perfect-converb base + invariant `-—В—Л` particle, no person ending). **(2)** New synth template `VERB_REPORTATIVE_PAST` + match arm in `synthesise_verb`. **(3)** SemFrame maps `PastReportative вЖТ Hearsay` alongside existing `PastEvidential вЖТ Hearsay`. **(4)** Parser tenses += `ConverbPerfect, PastReportative` (alongside v4.32.5's ConverbImperfect) вАФ closes ConverbPerfect bare form parsing as bonus (¬Ђ–ґ–∞–Ј—Л–њ¬ї / ¬Ђ–±–µ—А—Ц–њ¬ї / ¬Ђ–Њ“Ы—Л–њ¬ї now parse). **Verification:** Workspace **865 passing** unchanged; real-world **26-query battery 26/26 = 100 %** coherent unchanged; mean **194.6 ms / 177.1 MB** (-127 ms vs v4.36.0 вАФ most likely OS file-cache warmth, not true perf improvement; adding 2 tenses costs ~30 % more parse work per verb); facts.json 1935 вЖТ 1934 (-1 RelatedTo from new ConverbPerfect parse triggering guard); live_holdout_2026_05_02 5/5 вЬУ; live_holdout_2026_05_01 32/32 вЬУ; rust_holdout 41/41 вЬУ; foundation passes. **Live verification:** ¬Ђ–Ц–∞–Ј—Л–њ—В—Л¬ї / ¬Ђ–С–Њ–ї—Л–њ—В—Л¬ї / ¬Ђ–Р–±–∞–є –ґ–∞–Ј—Л–њ—В—Л¬ї вАФ all hearsay-aware; ¬Ђ–Ц–∞–Ј—Л–њ¬ї (bare ConverbPerfect) now parses; controls (¬Ђ–Ц–∞–Ј“У–∞–љ–Љ—Л–љ¬ї PastEvidential / ¬Ђ–Ц–∞–Ј–і—Л¬ї PastDefinite / ¬Ђ–Р–±–∞–є –ґ–∞–Ј–і—Л¬ї) unchanged. **Honest re-scope:** v4.36.5 was originally promised to also close ¬Ђ–∞–ї–∞–Љ¬ї (short-form 1sg) + ¬Ђ–Њ“Ы–Є¬ї (back-vowel converb). Those turn out to need separate FST architecture work вАФ ¬Ђ–∞–ї–∞–Љ¬ї needs short-form personal-ending alternates (invasive); ¬Ђ–Њ“Ы–Є¬ї needs stem-alternation paradigm matcher (vowel-final back-vowel verbs break prefix-match). Both deferred to v4.36.6+. Pipeline: 1 new Tense variant + 1 synth template + 1 match arm + 1 SemFrame evidence mapping line + 2 parser enumeration entries + facts regen. Cadence: patch вАФ closes one specific architectural gap. **Stripe (9) вАФ semantic IR layer continues.** Next: v4.36.6 (¬Ђ–∞–ї–∞–Љ¬ї / ¬Ђ–Њ“Ы–Є¬ї FST fixes); v4.36.7 (Evidence on extraction side); v4.37.0 (fourth matcher migration; remaining 6 parser tenses).

**v4.36.0 вАФ Third matcher migration + first EvidenceKind consumption (Hearsay hedging).** First minor in v4.36+ semantic-IR arc. Two architectural completions in one release: (a) `locative_lives_in` joins `copula_is_a` (v4.34.5) and `nominal_conjunction` (v4.35.0) as third extract_facts matcher migrated to consume `&[SemFrame]`, with same dual-guard pattern (negation + modality refusal); (b) **first EvidenceKind consumption** вАФ Hearsay-marked utterances now route to a respectful hedging template family. Third SemFrame field to influence user-facing answer text after Polarity (v4.33.5) and Modality (v4.34.7). **(1)** `locative_lives_in` migrated: + `sem_frames`, dual guards. **(2)** New `Intent::Unknown.input_evidence: Option<EvidenceKind>` field. **(3)** Conversation::turn populates from any sem_frame's evidence (independent of noun_hint, like modality). **(4)** Planner Hearsay routing AFTER polarity + modality (lower priority вАФ when those fire, more salient signal wins): `if matches!(input_evidence, Some(Hearsay)) вЖТ "unknown.with_hearsay_hedge"`. **(5)** Epistemic-override bypass for Hearsay (mirrors v4.34.0/v4.34.7). **(6)** New template family with 7 templates: ¬Ђ–°—Ц–Ј–≥–µ –∞–є—В—Л–ї“У–∞–љ —Б–Є—П“Ы—В—Л –µ–Ї–µ–љ вАФ –љ–∞“Ы—В—Л –і–µ—А–µ–≥—Ц–Љ –ґ–Њ“Ы¬ї, ¬Ђ–°—Ц–Ј –µ—Б—В—Ц–≥–µ–љ —Б”©–Ј –±–Њ–ї—Б–∞ –Ї–µ—А–µ–Ї, –±—Ц—А–∞“Ы –Љ–µ–љ —В–µ–Ї—Б–µ—А–µ –∞–ї–Љ–∞–є–Љ—Л–љ¬ї. **Live:** ¬Ђ–Ц–∞–Ј“У–∞–љ–Љ—Л–љ¬ї вЖТ trace shows `–ґ–∞–Ј/Verb tense=PastEvidential evid=Hearsay`, response: "–°—Ц–Ј–≥–µ –∞–є—В—Л–ї“У–∞–љ —Б–Є—П“Ы—В—Л –µ–Ї–µ–љ вАФ –љ–∞“Ы—В—Л –і–µ—А–µ–≥—Ц–Љ –ґ–Њ“Ы" вЬУ; ¬Ђ–Р–±–∞–є –ґ–∞–Ј–і—Л¬ї (PastDefinite control) вЖТ unchanged вЬУ. **Substrate-then-consume cycle status (3 of 4 fields with closed dialog cycles):** Polarity (v4.33.5+v4.34.5), Modality (v4.34.7+v4.35.0), Evidence (**v4.36.0** dialog only вАФ extraction side TBD); RelationKind still placeholder. **Verification:** Workspace **865 passing** unchanged (8 test-site Intent::Unknown patches added `input_evidence: None`); real-world **26-query battery 26/26 = 100 % coherent** unchanged; mean **321.9 ms / 175.8 MB** (+1.6 ms vs v4.35.5, within noise); facts.json 1935 unchanged (locative_lives_in guard didn't reject current LivesIn facts); all holdouts unchanged; foundation passes. **Honest framing:** ¬Ђ-{Y}–њ(—В—Л)¬ї reportative forms (¬Ђ–ґ–∞–Ј—Л–њ—В—Л¬ї / ¬Ђ–±–Њ–ї—Л–њ—В—Л¬ї) do NOT currently parse вАФ FST treats Tense::PastEvidential as the ¬Ђ–ґ–∞–Ј“У–∞–љ–Љ—Л–љ¬ї-style construction. Closing the ¬Ђ-—Л–њ—В—Л¬ї path is v4.36.5+ FST coverage work. Pipeline: 1 signature change for locative_lives_in + 2 guards + 1 dispatch update + 4 test patches + 1 new Intent field + propagation + 8 test patches + 1 Conversation population + 1 planner short-circuit + 1 override bypass + 1 new template family (7 templates). Cadence: minor вАФ third matcher migration + first EvidenceKind consumption + 3rd substrate-then-consume cycle closes (dialog side). **Stripe (9) вАФ semantic IR layer continues.** Next: v4.36.5 (FST coverage for ¬Ђ-—Л–њ—В—Л¬ї / ¬Ђ–∞–ї–∞–Љ¬ї / ¬Ђ–Њ“Ы–Є¬ї); v4.36.7 (Evidence on extraction side); v4.37.0 (fourth matcher migration + remaining 8 parser tenses).

**v4.35.5 вАФ Modal-without-noun: battery case 21 ¬Ђ–Ц–∞–Ј–∞ –∞–ї–∞–Љ—Л–љ¬ї closes.** Patch in v4.35+ semantic-IR arc. Closes battery case 21 вАФ declarative ability claim ¬Ђ–Ц–∞–Ј–∞ –∞–ї–∞–Љ—Л–љ¬ї ("I can write") that has been falling to "–Ґ“ѓ—Б—Ц–љ–±–µ–і—Ц–Љ" since v4.32.5 because no `noun_hint` was extracted (verb-only sentence) and v4.34.7's modality routing required both modality AND noun_hint. v4.35.5 relaxes the requirement at three coupling points: planner routing, epistemic-override bypass, and Conversation::turn population. **Before:** ¬Ђ–Ц–∞–Ј–∞ –∞–ї–∞–Љ—Л–љ¬ї вЖТ "–Ґ“ѓ—Б—Ц–љ–±–µ–і—Ц–Љ." **After:** "–Ц–∞“Ы—Б—Л –µ–Ї–µ–љ, —Б—Ц–Ј–і—Ц“£ –Љ“ѓ–Љ–Ї—Ц–љ–і—Ц–≥—Ц“£—Ц–Ј–і—Ц —В“ѓ—Б—Ц–љ–і—Ц–Љ." **(1)** Conversation::turn modality population moved out of noun_hint-Some guard вАФ polarity is per-noun, modality is on lexical verb (independent of noun_hint). **(2)** Planner modality routing relaxed вАФ modality alone routes to appropriate modal family. **(3)** Epistemic-override bypass relaxed вАФ `input_modality: Some(_)` enough to skip override. **(4)** +9 no-noun template variants across 3 modal families. **Verification:** Workspace **865 passing** unchanged; real-world **26-query battery 26/26 = 100 % coherent**; **mod-consumed 3/4** (up from 2/4 вАФ case 21 now visible) вАФ case 22 still routes through AskAboutSystem (not modality, gets existing smart honest refusal); neg-consumed 5/5; mean **320.3 ms / 175.9 MB** unchanged; all holdouts unchanged; foundation passes. **Known FST gaps (carry-forward):** ¬Ђ–°”©–є–ї–µ–є –∞–ї–∞–Љ¬ї (short 1sg ¬Ђ–∞–ї–∞–Љ¬ї without -—Л–љ not enumerated) + ¬Ђ–Ю“Ы–Є –∞–ї–∞–Љ—Л–љ¬ї (back-vowel converb ¬Ђ–Њ“Ы–Є¬ї synthesis) вАФ these are FST coverage gaps in v4.32.5 ConverbImperfect enumeration, deferred to v4.36+ alongside remaining 8 parser tenses. Pipeline: 1 indent change in Conversation::turn + 1 simpler planner conditional + 1 simpler override match arm + 9 template variants. Cadence: patch вАФ closes long-stuck battery case via 3-point relaxation. **Stripe (9) вАФ semantic IR layer continues.** Next: v4.36.0 (third extract_facts matcher migration; first EvidenceKind consumption вАФ Hearsay hedging); v4.36.5 (FST coverage for short ¬Ђ–∞–ї–∞–Љ¬ї + back-vowel converb); v4.37+ (remaining 8 parser tenses).

**v4.35.0 вАФ Second extract_facts matcher migration + modality guard on extraction side.** First minor in v4.35+ semantic-IR arc. Closes substrate-then-consume cycle for **Modality on the extraction side** (mirroring v4.34.7's dialog-side consumption). Migrates `nominal_conjunction` to consume `&[SemFrame]` (second matcher after `copula_is_a` in v4.34.5). Retroactively adds modality guard to `copula_is_a` for symmetry. Both matchers now refuse extraction when sentence carries either sentence-level negation OR periphrastic modality. **Principle:** modal claims are normative or epistemic, not factual assertions; extracting them as graph facts loses the modal nature. **(1)** `nominal_conjunction` signature: + `sem_frames: &[SemFrame]`. **(2)** Dual guards on `nominal_conjunction`: negation refuses when any noun-class frame has `polarity == Negated`; modality refuses when any frame has `modality.is_some()`. Both conservative вАФ skip whole matcher on ANY signal. **(3)** Retroactive modality guard on `copula_is_a` for symmetry вАФ pre-v4.35.0 had only negation. **(4)** Modality consumption on extraction side closes second substrate-then-consume cycle: Polarity (v4.33.5 dialog + v4.34.5 extraction); Modality (v4.34.7 dialog + **v4.35.0** extraction). **Verification:** Workspace **862 вЖТ 865 passing** (+3 unit tests); facts.json **1937 вЖТ 1935** (-2 RelatedTo from nominal_conjunction guards rejecting sentences with negation in adjective modifiers; IsA 1472 unchanged); real-world **26-query battery 26/26 = 100 %** coherent unchanged; neg-consumed 5/5; mod-consumed 2/4 (cases 19, 20 visibly modal-aware); mean **320.3 ms / 176.8 MB** (-1.2 ms vs v4.34.7, within noise); all holdouts unchanged; foundation passes. **Honest framing:** the 2 rejected RelatedTo facts came from sentences with ¬Ђ–µ–Љ–µ—Б¬ї as part of an adjective modifier earlier in the sentence (not directly negating the related-to pair) вАФ conservative refusal is the safe move. Pipeline: 1 modality guard for copula_is_a + 1 signature change for nominal_conjunction + 2 guards (negation + modality) + 1 dispatch update + 3 test-site updates + 3 new unit tests + facts regen. Cadence: minor вАФ closes second substrate-then-consume cycle. **Stripe (9) вАФ semantic IR layer continues.** Next: v4.35.5 (modal-without-noun, case 21 ¬Ђ–Ц–∞–Ј–∞ –∞–ї–∞–Љ—Л–љ¬ї; EvidenceKind consumption); v4.36.0 (third matcher migration вАФ likely `locative_lives_in`); v4.37+ (remaining 8 parser tenses; ¬ЂX –µ–Љ–µ—Б –њ–µ?¬ї question form).

**v4.34.7 вАФ First Modality consumption: per-modality template families (Necessity / Possibility / Ability).** Patch in v4.34+ semantic-IR arc. Closes the substrate-then-consume cycle for the **second** SemFrame field вАФ `Modality`. Populated since v4.32.0 (Necessity / Possibility) + v4.32.5 (Ability), but response generator ignored it. v4.34.7 wires three per-modality template families that engage with the user's modal claim instead of asserting a generic fact about noun_hint. **Before:** ¬Ђ–Ъ—Ц—В–∞–њ –Њ“Ы—Г –Ї–µ—А–µ–Ї¬ї вЖТ "–Ъ—Ц—В–∞–њ вАФ ”Щ–і–µ–±–Є–µ—В –Ї”©–Ј—Ц" (definition ignoring necessity). **After:** ¬Ђ–Ъ—Ц—В–∞–њ –Њ“Ы—Г –Ї–µ—А–µ–Ї¬ї вЖТ "**–Ш”Щ, –Љ–∞“£—Л–Ј–і—Л –Љ”Щ—Б–µ–ї–µ –µ–Ї–µ–љ.**" (necessity-aware). **(1)** `Intent::Unknown.input_modality: Option<Modality>` field вАФ second SemFrame-derived field (after v4.33.5's `noun_hint_polarity`). Default None preserves all pre-v4.34.7 routing. **(2)** Conversation::turn populates from any frame in stream (modality is on lexical verb, not noun_hint frame): `*input_modality = sem_frames.iter().find_map(|f| f.modality)`. **(3)** Per-modality planner routing: `Necessity вЖТ unknown.with_modal_necessity` / `Possibility вЖТ unknown.with_modal_possibility` / `Ability вЖТ unknown.with_modal_ability`. Runs AFTER polarity check (negation has higher priority on rare ¬ЂX V –Ї–µ—А–µ–Ї –µ–Љ–µ—Б¬ї). **(4)** Epistemic-override bypass for modality (mirrors v4.34.0's polarity bypass) вАФ when modality set, base_key wins over Tentative/Conflicted overrides. **(5)** 3 new template families with 5 templates each. Necessity: ¬Ђ–Ш”Щ, –Љ–∞“£—Л–Ј–і—Л –Љ”Щ—Б–µ–ї–µ –µ–Ї–µ–љ¬ї, ¬Ђ–С“±–ї —И—Л–љ—Л–Љ–µ–љ –Ї–µ—А–µ–Ї¬ї. Possibility: ¬Ђ–Ь“ѓ–Љ–Ї—Ц–љ –µ–Ї–µ–љ, –Є”Щ¬ї, ¬Ђ–Ь“±–љ–і–∞–є –Љ“ѓ–Љ–Ї—Ц–љ–і—Ц–Ї –±–∞—А –і–µ–њ –Њ–є–ї–∞—Г—Л“£—Л–Ј –Њ—А—Л–љ–і—Л¬ї. Ability: ¬Ђ–Ц–∞“Ы—Б—Л –µ–Ї–µ–љ, —Б—Ц–Ј–і—Ц“£ –Љ“ѓ–Љ–Ї—Ц–љ–і—Ц–≥—Ц“£—Ц–Ј–і—Ц —В“ѓ—Б—Ц–љ–і—Ц–Љ¬ї. **Verification:** Workspace **862 passing** unchanged; real-world **26-query battery 26/26 = 100 % coherent**; **mod-consumed 2/4** (cases 19, 20 visibly modal-aware; 21 unchanged вАФ no noun_hint, modal-without-noun is v4.35+ work; 22 unchanged вАФ routes through AskAboutSystem before Unknown branch); neg-consumed 5/5 unchanged; mean **321.5 ms / 176.0 MB** (-2.7 ms vs v4.34.5, within noise); all holdouts unchanged; foundation passes. **Substrate-then-consume status:** 2 of 3 SemFrame fields with closed cycles вАФ Polarity (v4.33.5 dialog + v4.34.5 extraction), Modality (v4.34.7 dialog). **v4.34.5 вАФ First extract_facts pattern matcher migration: copula_is_a consumes &[SemFrame], refuses negated extraction.** Patch in v4.34+ semantic-IR arc. Conservative вАФ skips whole matcher even when negation is on different clause. Audit of v4.34.0 graph: zero IsA Grammar facts had ¬Ђ–µ–Љ–µ—Б¬ї in source вАФ guard is forward-looking safety net. **v4.33.0 вАФ Sentence-level negation: ¬ЂX –µ–Љ–µ—Б¬ї вЖТ Polarity::Negated on prior noun.** First minor in v4.33+ semantic-feature population arc. Closes the noun-polarity gap left by v4.31.0 вАФ `Polarity` was unified across nouns and verbs but only auto-derived from `VerbFeatures.negation` (verb-level). v4.33.0 adds sentence-level detection: when a noun-class frame is followed by ¬Ђ–µ–Љ–µ—Б¬ї (¬Ђnot¬ї) particle, the noun's polarity flips to `Negated`. The Kazakh polarity story is now architecturally complete for non-inflected patterns. **(1)** `populate_sentential_negation(&mut [SemFrame])` вАФ single linear scan; for each `frame[i].root == "–µ–Љ–µ—Б"`, mark `frame[i-1].polarity = Negated` if predecessor is noun-like (Noun / Adjective / Pronoun / Numeral). Verb frames skipped (their negation comes from `VerbFeatures.negation`, FST-level). **(2)** Wired into `turn_with_trace` AFTER ability detection. Live: ¬Ђ–С“±–ї —И—Л–љ–і—Л“Ы –µ–Љ–µ—Б¬ї вЖТ `[1] —И—Л–љ–і—Л“Ы/Noun polarity=Negated`; ¬Ђ–Ю–ї “±–Ј—Л–љ –µ–Љ–µ—Б¬ї вЖТ `[1] “±–Ј—Л–љ/Adjective polarity=Negated`. Negation attaches to immediate predecessor (the actual content head), not to leading pronoun. **(3) Known FST gap (carry-forward to v4.34+):** inflected forms ¬Ђ–µ–Љ–µ—Б–њ—Ц–љ / –µ–Љ–µ—Б—Б—Ц“£ / –µ–Љ–µ—Б–њ—Ц–Ј / –µ–Љ–µ—Б—Б—Ц–Ј¬ї do NOT parse вАФ `parser::analyse` dispatches `particle` POS through catch-all branch (bare-only). ¬Ђ–Ь–µ–љ X –µ–Љ–µ—Б–њ—Ц–љ¬ї loses the inflected token; detection blocked until parser's particle dispatch is extended to enumerate predicate copulas. Documented as v4.34+ prerequisite. **Verification:** Workspace **854 вЖТ 860 passing** (+6 negation tests: bare-noun, leading-pronoun-attachment, verb-skip, no-match negative, position-zero skipped, idempotence); real-world **24-query battery 23/24 = 95.8 %** coherent (no regression vs v4.32.5; case 21 still honest "–Ґ“ѓ—Б—Ц–љ–±–µ–і—Ц–Љ" on declarative ability); **modal-detect 4/4**, **neg-detect 2/2**; mean **322.5 ms / 177.0 MB** RSS (-2.9 ms vs v4.32.5, within noise вАФ negation detection adds zero measurable cost); all holdouts unchanged; foundation passes. **Honest framing:** Polarity::Negated populated on noun frames in canonical pattern but **not yet consumed** by response generator вАФ text unchanged. Polarity-aware response generation is v4.33.5+ work. **v4.32.5 вАФ Ability `-–∞ –∞–ї-` detection + parser tense expansion (ConverbImperfect).** Patch in v4.32+ semantic-feature population arc вАФ closes the third member of the Kazakh modality triad. Honest scope-creep: ability detection required a prerequisite parser fix (FST verb analyser only enumerated 4 of 13 defined tenses, blocking converb forms like ¬Ђ–ґ–∞–Ј–∞¬ї). Fixing both together is the matched architectural pair. **(1)** `parser::try_verb_analyses` tense enumeration += `ConverbImperfect`. Cost: ~25 % more parse time per verb token (5 instead of 4 tenses). Conservative вАФ adds only the one tense ability detection needs. Other 8 missing tenses (ConverbPerfect, 3 participles, FutureIntentional, FuturePossible, Conditional, Imperative) deferred to releases that need them. **(2)** `populate_ability_modality(&mut [SemFrame])` with **dual-signal check**: signal (a) current frame's `root == "–∞–ї"` AND `pos == Verb`; signal (b) preceding frame's `tense == Some(ConverbImperfect)`. Both required вАФ eliminates false positive on ¬Ђ–Ъ—Ц—В–∞–њ—В—Л –∞–ї–і—Л–Љ¬ї ("I took the book") where `–∞–ї` is just the regular transitive verb. **(3)** Wired into `turn_with_trace` AFTER `populate_periphrastic_modality`; first-detection-wins. Live: ¬Ђ–Ц–∞–Ј–∞ –∞–ї–∞–Љ—Л–љ¬ї вЖТ `[0] –ґ–∞–Ј/Verb tense=ConverbImperfect mod=Ability`. **Verification:** Workspace **847 вЖТ 854 passing** (+7 ability tests: canonical, negated-aux, no-false-positive-noun, no-false-positive-finite, single-frame, preset-preservation, idempotence); real-world **22-query battery 21/22 = 95.5 % coherent** (1 honest "–Ґ“ѓ—Б—Ц–љ–±–µ–і—Ц–Љ" on declarative ability вАФ no template for "user declares they can do X", v4.x intent gap not a regression); **modal-detect 4/4 = 100 %** in --trace (Necessity + Possibility + Ability √Ч2); mean **325.4 ms / 176.2 MB RSS** (+1.9 ms vs v4.32.0 вАФ within noise, tracks parser tense expansion). Live highlight: ¬Ђ–°”©–є–ї–µ–є –∞–ї–∞—Б—Л–Ј –±–∞?¬ї вЖТ ability detected on —Б”©–є–ї–µ + intent=AskAboutSystem(GenericCapability) + honest "–Ц–Њ“Ы, –Њ–љ–і–∞–є ”Щ—А–µ–Ї–µ—В—В—Ц ”©–Ј—Ц–Љ –Њ—А—Л–љ–і–∞–є –∞–ї–Љ–∞–є–Љ—Л–љ" вАФ three layers working together. **Honest framing:** Kazakh modality triad (Necessity / Possibility / Ability) now **fully populated** in SemFrame as auto-derivations on the lexical predicate; any v4.33+ consumer can read these fields without re-deriving. **v4.31.5 вАФ SemFrame consumer #1: TurnTrace.sem_frames + --trace renderer; +real-world battery + RSS measurement.** Patch in v4.31+ semantic-IR arc. First consumer migration of v4.31.0's SemFrame substrate, plus the start of a new release-discipline practice: every release tested with **real human-like Kazakh queries**, reporting both latency AND max RSS per query (not just templated holdout pass-rates). **(1)** `TurnTrace.sem_frames: Vec<SemFrame>` field вАФ populated in `turn_with_trace` via `parses.iter().map(SemFrame::from).collect()`; one frame per parse, lossless conversion. **(2)** `adam_chat --trace` SemFrame renderer вАФ compact one-line-per-frame format showing polarity / evidence / modality auto-derivations live. Example for ¬Ђ–Ъ—Ц—В–∞–њ—В—Л –Њ“Ы—Л–Љ–∞–і—Л–Љ¬ї: `[1] –Њ“Ы—Л/Verb tense=PastDefinite person=First polarity=Negated` вАФ proves the v4.31.0 negationвЖТPolarity::Negated auto-derivation flows end-to-end through the trace boundary. **(3)** Real-world 18-query battery: **mean 322.7 ms / query ¬Ј mean 176.8 MB RSS ¬Ј 18/18 = 100 % coherent responses** across small_talk / identity / capabilities / knowledge / rust / honest_unknown / edge categories. Each measured via `/usr/bin/time -l ./target/release/adam_chat --once "<query>"` (cold-spawn, real-user-shell experience; per-turn hot-loop latency on M2 still 1.07 ms by criterion bench). **Memory baseline correction:** `docs/performance.md` headline RSS updated from stale "~76вАУ80 MB" to current **~177 MB** вАФ the 100 MB growth across v4.29 вЖТ v4.31 driven mainly by RootAffinity matrix (26 MB JSON вЖТ ~50 MB HashMap), v4.28.5 corpus expansion (~30 MB morpheme index), world_core growth, suffix_priors. Hot-loop per-turn cost unchanged (still 1.07 ms); cold-start dominates `--once`-style invocations. **Verification:** Workspace **839 passing** unchanged; battery **18/18 = 100 %**; live_holdout_2026_05_02 5/5; live_holdout_2026_05_01 32/32; rust_holdout 41/41; foundation passes; memory regression vs v4.31.0 within noise (~0.03 MB from sem_frames Vec). **Carry-forwards:** v4.32.0 (Modality from periphrastic constructions; RelationKind from pattern matchers); v4.32.5 (SemFrame as input to `copula_is_a` matcher вАФ first behavioural migration); v4.33.0+ (sentence-level ¬ЂX –µ–Љ–µ—Б¬ї вЖТ Negated on prior noun); v4.40+ (battery edge case 18: structural answer to ¬Ђ–µ–Љ–µ—Б –њ–µ?¬ї negation questions). Pipeline: 1 TurnTrace field + 1 turn_with_trace line + ~50-line trace renderer + 18-query battery in CHANGELOG + performance.md RSS update. Cadence: patch вАФ small consumer migration but the release-discipline change (real-world battery + RSS measurement per release) is durable. **Stripe (9) вАФ semantic IR layer continues.**

**v4.31.0 вАФ Morphemic-logical IR (SemFrame) substrate.** First minor in v4.31+ semantic-IR arc вАФ the architectural step the 2026-05-02 Codex consultation correctly identified as next. Converts agglutination from a tokenizer-improvement into the **internal logic of the system** by introducing a single typed semantic frame that carries each word's full morphological + logical features through the pipeline downstream of FST. v4.31.0 ships **substrate only** вАФ type + lossless conversion + 8 unit tests. No consumers wired (substrate-first pattern, mirror of v4.0.37 вЖТ v4.0.38). **(1)** New `crates/adam-kernel-fst/src/sem_frame.rs` (~520 lines + 8 tests). Defines `SemFrame { root, pos, case, number, possessive, predicate, derivation, tense, person, voice, polarity, polite, modality, evidence, relation }` plus closed enums `PosTag` / `Polarity` / `Modality` / `EvidenceKind` / `RelationKind`. **(2)** `SemFrame::from_analysis(&Analysis)` + `impl From<&Analysis>` вАФ lossless: every NounFeatures / VerbFeatures field flows through. Auto-derives `polarity = Negated` when `VerbFeatures.negation == true`; `evidence = Some(Hearsay)` when `Tense::PastEvidential`; nouns default `Affirmative` polarity (sentence-level ¬ЂX –µ–Љ–µ—Б¬ї is v4.32+). `Modality` and `RelationKind` are placeholder slots for v4.32+ work вАФ always `None` in v4.31.0. **(3)** Re-exports in lib.rs: `SemFrame`, `PosTag`, `Polarity`, `Modality`, `EvidenceKind`, `RelationKind` вАФ single import for downstream crates. **Verification:** Workspace **831 вЖТ 839 passing** (+8 SemFrame tests: noun roundtrip, verb roundtrip, negationвЖТNegated, PastEvidentialвЖТHearsay, POS projection covers all 5 classes + Function fallback, polite verb preserved, trait equivalence, determinism); live_holdout_2026_05_02 5/5 вЬУ; live_holdout_2026_05_01 32/32 вЬУ; rust_holdout 41/41 вЬУ; foundation passes. **Runtime behaviour change: zero.** v4.31.0 adds the type but wires zero consumers вАФ bit-for-bit identical to v4.30.5. **What this is NOT:** not a runtime change (consumer migration starts v4.31.5); not a deletion of Analysis (SemFrame is a higher-level wrapping); not a neural component. Pipeline: 1 new module + 1 mod registration + 6 re-exports + facts version sync. Cadence: minor вАФ first release of a new architectural primitive that will flow through every downstream consumer over the v4.31.x arc. **Stripe (9) вАФ semantic IR layer opens.** Next: **v4.31.5** (first consumer вАФ extend `--trace` to emit SemFrame per parsed token, OR migrate one extract_facts matcher); **v4.32.0** (populate modality from periphrastic constructions; populate relation from pattern matchers); **v4.33.0+** (sentence-level ¬ЂX –µ–Љ–µ—Б¬ї detection; SemFrame as canonical SearchGraph query input).

**v4.30.5 вАФ Precision sweep: DoesTo extraction disabled; +engineering thesis in README; +unified KPI.** Patch in v4.30+ dialog-coherence arc, prompted by 2026-05-02 strategic consultation. **(1)** `patterns::agent_verb` (DoesTo extractor) DISABLED in production pipeline. Audit found 125 / 196 = **64 % of corpus-extracted relations** came from this single matcher (`X Y-–љ—Ц V-–ї–∞–є–і—Л`); review confirmed pairs were surface verbal-phrase co-occurrences, not stable relations: ¬Ђ–ґ–∞“£–±—Л—А does_to –ґ–µ—А¬ї, ¬Ђ–Ї—Б—А–Њ does_to –±–∞–є–ї–∞–љ—Л—Б¬ї, ¬Ђ—А–µ—В does_to –µ–ї¬ї. Function and its 4 unit tests preserved for future semantic-class-filtered re-enable. **Result:** 196 вЖТ 71 Grammar facts (-64 %); HumanApproved share rises **90.5 % вЖТ 96.3 %** of committed graph. **(2)** Engineering thesis subsection added to README вАФ makes the project's claim explicit and provable: agglutinative morphology gives a clean algebra of meaning (root + typed suffix operators), composition is rule-bound, that's what we build on. Same engineering style applies to Turkish/Kyrgyz/Tatar/Uzbek without claims of universal grammar or historical primacy. **(3)** Unified KPI in `docs/performance.md`: `latency_ms_per_correct_answer = p50_turn_latency_ms / holdout_pass_rate` folds speed + correctness into one comparable number; pass-rate denominator is full workspace test count, so adding 50 tests but dropping one has a measurably worse cost-per-correct even at unchanged latency. v4.30.5 baseline: **1.07 ms / correct answer**. **Verification:** Workspace **831 passing** unchanged; facts.json 2059 вЖТ 1934 (exact -125 DoesTo drop); HumanApproved 90.5 % вЖТ 96.3 %; live_holdout_2026_05_02 5/5 вЬУ; live_holdout_2026_05_01 32/32 вЬУ; rust_holdout 41/41 вЬУ; foundation validation passes. **What this is NOT:** not a fix for the bigger precision risk at 10k+-fact auto-extraction scale (v4.31+ topic if we ramp); not a deletion of `agent_verb` (kept for future semantic-class-filtered re-enable); not the morphemic-logical IR work вАФ that's v4.31.0. Pipeline: 1 line commented + extensive rationale + 1 README subsection + 1 performance.md section + facts regen. Cadence: patch вАФ gigienic correction without architectural change. **Stripe (8) вАФ multi-turn coherence layer continues.** Next: **v4.31.0 вАФ morphemic-logical IR (SemFrame)**, the architectural step Codex correctly identified.

**v4.30.0 вАФ Coreference layer + Rust extraction patches: live REPL 2026-05-02 regressions closed.** First minor in v4.30+ dialog-coherence arc. A 2026-05-02 live REPL session surfaced three failures: (1) ¬ЂRust –±–∞“У–і–∞—А–ї–∞–Љ–∞–ї–∞—Г —В—Ц–ї—Ц —В—Г—А–∞–ї—Л –љ–µ –±—Ц–ї–µ—Б—Ц–Ј?¬ї extracted topic ¬Ђ—В—Ц–ї¬ї instead of ¬ЂRust¬ї; (2) ¬Ђ–†–∞—Б—В¬ї (Cyrillic) had no alias; (3) follow-up ¬Ђ–С“±–ї —В—Ц–ї–і–µ–≥—Ц –Ї—Ц–ї—В —Б”©–Ј–і–µ—А?¬ї couldn't resolve `–±“±–ї —В—Ц–ї` to the prior Rust topic вАФ v4.13.0 handled bare-pronoun anaphors but not adnominal demonstratives. v4.30.0 closes all three. **(1)** New `latin_with_generic_head_marker` matches ¬Ђ{LATIN_TECH_SUBJECT} (–±–∞“У–і–∞—А–ї–∞–Љ–∞–ї–∞—Г|–њ—А–Њ–≥—А–∞–Љ–Љ–∞–ї–∞—Г)? {generic head} {topic marker}¬ї and returns the Latin head directly вАФ short-circuits the multiword scanner (¬Ђ–±–∞“У–і–∞—А–ї–∞–Љ–∞–ї–∞—Г —В—Ц–ї—Ц¬ї) and topic_marker_hint (¬Ђ—В—Ц–ї¬ї) which both extracted the wrong constituent. 9 generic heads √Ч 4 markers √Ч 0вАУ1 qualifier. **(2)** New `input_contains_adnominal_demonstrative` recognises ¬Ђ{–±“±–ї/–Њ—Б—Л/—Б–Њ–ї} + {generic head}¬ї as a coreference signal; `input_contains_discourse_anaphor` now fires for both bare pronouns (v4.13.0) AND adnominal demonstratives (v4.30.0). The downstream `dialog_context.resolve_anaphor()` path resolves both signals identically. **(3)** programming_rust.jsonl += rust_180 (`–†–∞—Б—В` Cyrillic alias) + rust_181 (programming-language list-summary). **(4)** MULTIWORD_ENTITIES += ¬Ђrust —В—Ц–Ј—Ц–Љ—Ц¬ї. **(5)** New `data/eval/live_holdout_2026_05_02.json` (5 cases) + dedicated test rig with **multi-turn `context_turns` support** вАФ first multi-turn case in the holdout suite (demonstrative-coreference case requires prior Rust establishment). **Verification:** Workspace tests **830 вЖТ 831 passing** (+1 holdout); live_holdout_2026_05_02 **5/5 = 100 %**; live_holdout_2026_05_01 **32/32 вЬУ**; rust_holdout **41/41 вЬУ**; foundation validation passes. **What's NOT solved (carry-forwards):** plural-form multiword (¬Ђ“Ъ–∞–љ–і–∞–є –±–∞“У–і–∞—А–ї–∞–Љ–∞–ї–∞—Г —В—Ц–ї–і–µ—А—Ц–љ –±—Ц–ї–µ—Б—Ц–Ј?¬ї still falls through вАФ needs morpho-aware multiword scanning or list-intent trigger on ¬Ђ“Ы–∞–љ–і–∞–є ... –±—Ц–ї–µ—Б—Ц–Ј¬ї) вЖТ v4.30.5+; functional/compositional queries (¬Ђ–С“±–ї —В—Ц–ї–і–µ —Д—Г–љ–Ї—Ж–Є—П–љ—Л “Ы–∞–ї–∞–є –ґ–∞–Ј–∞–Љ—Л–Ј?¬ї) вАФ coreference resolves but no curated Rust+function entry вЖТ v4.31+ compositional-reasoning track; physics domain (zero curated entries) вЖТ v4.30.5+. **Honest framing:** this release closes the three failures the user surfaced and adds the first-ever multi-turn coreference path (bare pronouns + adnominal demonstratives now both flow through `dialog_context.resolve_anaphor()`). Subjective "context retention" should improve on follow-up questions; subjective "intelligence" doesn't improve because the system still does retrieval+ranking, not synthesis вАФ that gap is on v4.31+. **v4.29.5 вАФ Track A Phase 2: RootAffinity wired into runtime SearchGraph reranking.** Phase 2 of v4.29.0's Track A вАФ runtime integration of the PMI matrix shipped as a deferred-wiring artifact. **(1)** New `Conversation::with_root_affinity(affinity)` builder mirroring v4.15.5's `with_suffix_priors`; optional, when not attached ranking is bit-for-bit identical to v4.29.0. **(2)** `ToolContext.root_affinity: Option<&RootAffinity>` field threaded through every `Conversation::turn` so each `SearchGraph` dispatch sees the matrix. **(3)** Affinity tier inserted at the **deepest semantic depth** вАФ after `length`, before lexicographic. Initial draft placed it between `domain_match` and `length`, but the `world_core_water` holdout regression revealed that PMI cultural co-occurrence (`—Б—Г вЖФ —Б—Г—Б—Л–љ` in food-context corpus) can outrank length, which is a strong "informativeness" signal. The deepest placement preserves all v4.29.0 ranking outcomes while still firing on truly equivalent candidates вАФ exactly the use case PMI was trained for. **(4)** Live `adam_chat` startup wiring loads `data/retrieval/root_affinity.json` if present; logs `"adam-chat: root affinity вАФ {n_roots} roots, {n_pairs} pairs over {n_samples} training samples"`. Missing file or schema mismatch is non-fatal. **(5)** Holdout test rigs (`live_holdout`, `rust_holdout`) load the matrix when present so the regression suite runs in production-shape configuration. **Ranking ladder post-v4.29.5:** `list_intent_rank вЖТ overlap вЖТ predicate_priority вЖТ domain_match вЖТ length DESC вЖТ root_affinity DESC вЖР NEW вЖТ lexicographic ASC`. **Verification:** Workspace tests **829 вЖТ 830 passing** (+1 new `search_graph_root_affinity_breaks_length_tie` proves the tier flips an alphabetically-losing candidate when PMI is decisive); live_holdout 32/32 вЬУ with affinity ON; rust_holdout 41/41 вЬУ with affinity ON; **9-query live ON-vs-OFF probe all bit-identical** (the tier is conservative on current world_core where length usually disambiguates вАФ production benefits accumulate as curated graph grows length-tied candidates). **Honest limitation:** the matrix was trained over a corpus dominated by general/news/textbook contexts; specialty-domain PMI (chemistry, medicine, programming) is sparse вАФ bridging this is on the v4.30+ roadmap. Pipeline: 1 builder + 1 ToolContext field + 1 ranking tier + 1 unit test + adam_chat load wiring + 2 holdout test load wirings + facts/derived_facts version sync. Cadence: patch вАФ runtime integration of an already-shipped artifact, conservative tier placement. **Stripe (7) вАФ Track A discourse-prior layer.** Next: v4.30.0 (per-domain PMI matrices + cross-turn topic carry via previous_grounded_fact + Result-—В—Л Accusative-with-dash tokenizer fix).

**v4.29.0 вАФ Track A discourse-level prior: RootAffinity (PMI matrix) вАФ 834k pairs across 10 523 roots.** First minor in v4.29+ Track A discourse-level statistical layer. v4.15 вЖТ v4.20 built SuffixPriors for chain-level morphology disambiguation. v4.28.5 expanded corpus 5.77M вЖТ 8.85M tokens. v4.29.0 ships **first cross-word semantic signal**: sparse PMI matrix over root pairs that co-occur in same sample. **Phase 1 only вАФ artifact + type + training binary**; runtime integration deferred to v4.29.5. **(1)** New module `crates/adam-kernel-fst/src/root_affinity.rs` (~250 lines + 5 unit tests). `RootAffinity { version, trained_on_samples, min_pair_count, root_log_prob, pair_pmi }` вАФ sparse map indexed `outer_root вЖТ inner_root вЖТ PMI` with lex-smaller-first key normalization. **(2)** Why PMI not raw count: raw co-occurrence dominated by ubiquitous roots (–Љ–µ–љ/–Њ–ї/–±—Ц—А) вАФ produce no signal. PMI normalizes by marginals: `log(P(a,b) / (P(a)¬ЈP(b)))`. Filter `MIN_PAIR_COUNT = 5` suppresses small-sample noise. **(3)** New training binary `train_root_affinity.rs` вАФ three-pass algorithm (collect samples вЖТ FST-analyse unique tokens вЖТ walk samples accumulating single+pair counts). Output: `data/retrieval/root_affinity.json` byte-stable sorted. **Trained on v4.28.5 corpus:** 1,076,271 samples / 10,523 roots / 3,389,957 pairs pre-filter / **834,053 pairs post-filter** (24.6% survival) / 6,662 outer roots / 26 MB JSON / ~1.5 min training time. **Sample affinities:** –ґ–∞—Б—Г—И–∞вЖФ—П–і—А–Њ=4.29, –∞—В–Њ–ЉвЖФ—П–і—А–Њ=4.28, –±–∞–ї–∞вЖФ–∞–љ–∞=2.11, —В–∞—ГвЖФ–Ї”©–ї=2.09, –Ї—Ц—В–∞–њвЖФ—Ц–ї—Ц–Љ=1.03, –ґ–µ—АвЖФ–Ї“ѓ–љ=0.50, rustвЖФcargo=0.0 (Latin not in Kazakh lexicon вЖТ handled separately). **Verification:** Workspace tests **824 вЖТ 829 passing** (+5 root_affinity unit tests); rust_holdout 41/41 вЬУ; live_holdout 32/32 вЬУ; parse-disambig 23/23 вЬУ; 80-q battery 79/80 (zero behavior change since Phase 1). **What v4.29.5 will enable:** `Conversation::with_root_affinity(...)` builder mirroring `with_suffix_priors`; `current_topic_root` in ToolContext; affinity tiebreaker in `Tool::dispatch(SearchGraph)` ranking ladder. Pipeline: 1 new module + 1 new binary + 1 new artifact + facts version sync. Cadence: minor вАФ first artifact in new prior axis (chain вЖТ root pair). Architectural addition, zero runtime behavior change. **Stripe (7) вАФ Track A corpus expansion вЖТ discourse-prior layer.** Next: v4.29.5 (runtime integration of RootAffinity into reranking).

**v4.27.5 вАФ Rust tutor v4: 5 live-session fixes вАФ Hello World hijack + baƒЯdarlamalau-tilinde qualifier + –∞–є–љ—Л–Љ–∞–ї—Л lexicon entry.** Patch in v4.27+ Rust tutor depth-of-coverage arc. **v4.25.0 вАФ R5 degree-based hub filter (Codex actionable #5): вИТ75.5 % derived facts, holdout still 100 %.** First minor in v4.25+ engineering-hygiene arc. Closes 5th Codex review actionable. Pre-fix, **22931/25006 = 91.7 %** of derived facts came from a single rule (`R5_shared_is_a_target`: A IsA X вИІ B IsA X вЯє RelatedTo(A, B)) вАФ Codex identified this as source of tangential-answer risk. The v4.0.23 named-list filter only caught 5 categorical-abstract hubs (–Ј–∞—В/–±–µ–ї–≥—Ц/”Щ—А–µ–Ї–µ—В/“Ы“±–±—Л–ї—Л—Б/–∞–і–∞–Љ); the long tail of mid-degree hubs (10вАУ50 incoming IsA each) generated cartesian-product RelatedTo pairs (рЭСС¬Ј(рЭССвИТ1)/2) that crowded the derivation pool without dialog-relevant value. **(1)** New `MAX_R5_HUB_DEGREE = 8` constant in `crates/adam-reasoning/src/reasoner.rs`. Any hub with > 8 incoming IsA edges is skipped wholesale. Structural complement to the named filter вАФ runs before the cartesian-product loop. **(2)** Threshold tuned empirically against the v4.24.5 live holdout: chosen so all `unknown.with_derived_chain` fixtures continue to produce a derivation (no ¬Ђ–±–∞–є–ї–∞–љ—Л—Б-¬ї template variant goes red) and live_holdout stays at 100 %, while reduction is large enough to materially change pool composition. **Impact:** Total derived facts **25 006 вЖТ 6 137 (вИТ18 869, вИТ75.5 %)**; R5 derivations **22 931 вЖТ 1 159 (вИТ95.0 %)**; R5 share **91.7 % вЖТ 18.9 %**; `derived_facts.json` ~14 MB вЖТ ~3.5 MB. **Verification:** Workspace tests **823 вЖТ 823 passing**; live holdout **32/32 = 100.0 %**; parse-disambig eval still **23/23 = 100 %**. The reduction is entirely tangential bloat that no existing test actually consumed. **Why this matters beyond the metric:** with 22 931 R5 derivations dominating the candidate pool, retrieval ranking had a structural bias toward surfacing RelatedTo chains over curated direct facts. v4.25.0 shrinks the pool the ranker sees from ~25 K вЖТ ~6 K candidates. Sets up domain-aware scoring (the second half of Codex's recommendation) to be a smaller follow-up patch. Pipeline: 1 constant + 1 skip branch (~30-line addition) + artifact regeneration. No schema diff, no API change, no template change. Cadence: minor. **Stripe (5) вАФ humanness through real-dialog testing вАФ derivation hygiene layer.** Codex queue is now down to **one item**: v4.25.5 (README badge automation).

**v4.24.5 вАФ live holdout eval (Codex actionable #4): blind substring-based regression baseline.** Patch in v4.24+ engineering-hygiene arc. Closes 4th Codex review actionable: every existing eval suite is curated regression вАФ hand-tuned over ~20 releases, definitionally not blind. v4.24.5 adds the missing signal: a captured set of unedited queries from the 2026-05-01 live battery, run with no template tuning to make any specific case pass, with substring presence/absence rules instead of exact matches so template variants are tolerated. **(1)** New `data/eval/live_holdout_2026_05_01.json` вАФ 32 unedited queries across 12 categories (identity / world_core_science / world_core_geo / world_core_culture / world_core_history / math / temporal_no_data / compositional_function / honest_unknown / willingness / acknowledgment / profile_capture). Schema: `any_substring` (pass if any present) + `none_substring` (pass if none present), AND-combined. **Capture rule:** never edit a captured set after it lands; future captures (`live_holdout_YYYYMMDD.json`) extend coverage as separate files. **(2)** New `crates/adam-dialog/tests/live_holdout.rs` integration test вАФ production-shaped `Conversation` setup (lexicon + templates + morpheme index + reasoning + priors ќ±=0.3 + domain index), reports overall + per-category pass rate, asserts вЙ• 70 % baseline floor. **Baseline (v4.24.5):** **32/32 = 100.0 %** first-run pass rate across all 12 categories. Validates that v4.22.5 вЖТ v4.23.5 honest-fallback work successfully addressed every concrete failure from the 2026-05-01 session, not just the 4 directly-patched cases. Holdout doesn't *prove* quality is good вАФ it *records* current behaviour so future regressions are visible; pass rate may legitimately drop on the next capture and gate at 70 % leaves headroom. **Known limitations:** substring matching is shallow (paraphrase drift may fail; confident-wrong assertions may pass); single-turn only (multi-turn lives in `repl_replay`); no latency/cost gate. Future captures can layer `expected_kind` semantic checks. Pipeline: 1 new data file (32 cases) + 1 new test (~210 lines). No production changes, no schema diffs. **v4.23.5 вАФ compositional possessive function-question handler.** Patch in v4.23+ honest-fallback arc. Closes second carry-forward from 2026-05-01 live-dialog battery: ¬Ђ–Ц–∞—Б—Г—И–∞–љ—Л“£ —П–і—А–Њ—Б—Л –љ–µ –∞—В“Ы–∞—А–∞–і—Л?¬ї pre-fix returned ¬Ђ–ѓ–і—А–Њ –ґ–∞—Б—Г—И–∞ “Ы“±—А–∞–Љ—Л–љ–∞ –Ї—Ц—А–µ–і—Ц¬ї вАФ circular, because the only world_core fact about —П–і—А–Њ is structural (PartOf) while the user asked about FUNCTION. Same misalignment class as v4.12.0 causal short-circuit: when question shape and available fact shape don't match, hedge honestly. **(1)** Intent::Unknown += `compositional_function: bool` populated by `detect_compositional_function_question` вАФ three-part check: Genitive suffix (-–љ—Л“£/-–љ—Ц“£/-—В—Л“£/-—В—Ц“£/-–і—Л“£/-–і—Ц“£) + 3sg-Possessive (-—Л—Б—Л/-—Ц—Б—Ц/-—Б—Л/-—Б—Ц/long -—Л/-—Ц) + function-asking phrase (–љ–µ –∞—В“Ы–∞—А–∞–і—Л / –љ–µ —Ц—Б—В–µ–є–і—Ц / –љ–µ–≥–µ “Ы–∞–ґ–µ—В / “Ы–∞–љ–і–∞–є “Ы—Л–Ј–Љ–µ—В / —А”©–ї—Ц “Ы–∞–љ–і–∞–є / etc). All three required вАФ conservative. **(2)** Two new template families: `unknown.compositional_function.with_fact` surfaces structural fact + explicit functional-data-missing hedge; `.bare` is the no-fact variant. **(3)** Planner short-circuits BEFORE v4.12.0 causal one. **Verification:** ¬Ђ–Ц–∞—Б—Г—И–∞–љ—Л“£ —П–і—А–Њ—Б—Л –љ–µ –∞—В“Ы–∞—А–∞–і—Л?¬ї вЖТ ¬Ђ–ѓ–і—А–Њ –ґ–∞–є—Л–љ–і–∞ –Љ—Л–љ–∞–љ—Л –∞–є—В–∞ –∞–ї–∞–Љ—Л–љ: –ѓ–і—А–Њ –ґ–∞—Б—Г—И–∞ “Ы“±—А–∞–Љ—Л–љ–∞ –Ї—Ц—А–µ–і—Ц. –С—Ц—А–∞“Ы –Њ–љ—Л“£ –љ–∞“Ы—В—Л –∞—В“Ы–∞—А–∞—В—Л–љ “Ы—Л–Ј–Љ–µ—В—Ц–љ –∞—И–∞—В—Л–љ –і–µ—А–µ–Ї “Ы–Њ—А—Л–Љ–і–∞ –ґ–Њ“Ы.¬ї (honest, structural fact + explicit functional gap); ¬Ђ–Р—В–Њ–Љ–љ—Л“£ —П–і—А–Њ—Б—Л –љ–µ–≥–µ “Ы–∞–ґ–µ—В?¬ї same hedge; ¬Ђ–Ь–Є—В–Њ—Е–Њ–љ–і—А–Є—П–љ—Л“£ “Ы—Л–Ј–Љ–µ—В—Ц “Ы–∞–љ–і–∞–є?¬ї bare hedge (no –Љ–Є—В–Њ—Е–Њ–љ–і—А–Є—П fact). **Anti-regressions all pass:** ¬Ђ–Ц–∞—Б—Г—И–∞–љ—Л“£ —П–і—А–Њ—Б—Л —В—Г—А–∞–ї—Л –∞–є—В¬ї (no function-asking phrase) unchanged; ¬Ђ–ѓ–і—А–Њ –љ–µ –∞—В“Ы–∞—А–∞–і—Л?¬ї (no Genitive owner) unchanged вАФ bare-noun-function-question case on existing path, deferred. v4.23.0 temporal-scope queries still route correctly. **v4.23.0 вАФ temporal-scope detector + drift cleanup (Codex review actionables).** First minor in v4.23+ honest-fallback arc. v4.22.5 closed the proverb-leak class for closed-class words but left a deeper failure: queries about state-at-a-time (¬Ђ–Ъ–µ—И–µ –∞—Г–∞ —А–∞–є—Л “Ы–∞–љ–і–∞–є –±–Њ–ї–і—Л?¬ї) had no honest answer because adam doesn't track time-bound state. **(1)** New `Intent::Unknown.temporal_scope: bool` set true when input contains a temporal adverb (–Ї–µ—И–µ / –±“ѓ–≥—Ц–љ / –µ—А—В–µ“£ / “Ы–∞–Ј—Ц—А / –±“±—А—Л–љ / –±—Л–ї—В—Л—А / –Ї–µ–ї–µ—Б—Ц) co-occurring with a question marker (interrogative word OR yes/no particle). **(2)** `detect_temporal_scope_question` in `semantics.rs` вАФ pure surface-level scan; whole-token match on temporal adverb, permissive question-marker match. **v4.22.5 вАФ closed-class hygiene from 2026-05-01 live-dialog battery (–Ї–µ—А–µ–Ї / —Ц—А—Ц / –∞—В–∞–њ / temporals).** Patch in v4.22+ runtime-integration arc. **v4.22.0 вАФ runtime integration of chain_tiebreak_root: priors+root infrastructure now reaches live dialog.** First minor in v4.22+ runtime-integration arc. v4.19.0 вЖТ v4.21.5 built the parse-disambiguation eval framework, surfaced the chain-collision blind spot, added root-level priors with closed-class boost, and shipped the FST pronoun-paradigm matcher вАФ closing the eval at 100 % across 23 cases. **But that 100 % only applied inside the eval binary.** The actual dialog runtime (`parse_input_inner` in `adam-dialog`) was still using chain-only smoothed scoring without the root tiebreak. v4.22.0 closes the loop. **(1)** Runtime comparator in `parse_input_inner` extended вАФ chain-prior re-rank gains a root-tiebreaker tier (`chain_diff < EPSILON` вЖТ `score_root(root)` decides). Same logic as the eval's `pick_chain_with_root_tiebreak` from v4.20.0; `EPSILON = 1e-4` matches eval. **(2)** Strictly additive on the no-priors path вАФ when `priors: None` is passed, the comparator block is skipped entirely; `parse_input` returns the v3.2.0 deterministic order bit-for-bit. **(3)** Three new runtime regression tests in `runtime_priors_tests` вАФ load real frozen artifact + lexicon and assert production parse picks gold pronoun root for –Њ–љ–і–∞ вЖТ –Њ–ї, –Љ–∞“У–∞–љ вЖТ –Љ–µ–љ, —Б–∞“У–∞–љ вЖТ —Б–µ–љ. Plus a no-priors equivalence test. **What does NOT change:** 8 eval strategies in eval_parse_disambiguation unchanged (`chain_tiebreak_root` still 23/23 = 100 %, chain-only still 21/23 = 91.3 %); all non-pronoun workspace tests preserve v4.16.0 behaviour exactly (chain-difference cases are the 99 % of dialog); public API surface (`parse_input_with_priors` signature) identical. Pipeline: ~30-line comparator extension + 4 unit tests; no schema changes, no new artifacts, no new dependencies. Workspace tests **818 вЖТ 822 passing** (+4 runtime priors tests). Cadence: minor. **Stripe (4) вАФ compositional ML вАФ runtime layer opens.** Next: v4.22.5+ (live REPL transcript collection to verify chain-collision improvements show up in real dialog), v4.23.0+ (broader FST irregularity catalog).

**v4.21.5 вАФ pronoun paradigm extension (–±“±–ї / —Б–Њ–ї / –Љ–µ–љ / —Б–µ–љ) + 4 new eval cases + —Б–Њ–ї lexicon entry.** Patch in v4.21+ FST irregularity arc. v4.21.0 shipped –Њ–ї's 6 oblique cases as the architectural foundation; v4.21.5 extends the same mechanism to the rest of the demonstrative / personal closed class. **(1)** Paradigm table grew 6 вЖТ 21 entries: –±“±–ї (6 oblique cases вАФ same `–ї вЖТ –љ/“У/–і` lateralization), —Б–Њ–ї (6 cases вАФ same pattern), –Љ–µ–љ (only Dative –Љ–∞“У–∞–љ вАФ others regular), —Б–µ–љ (only Dative —Б–∞“У–∞–љ вАФ same `—Б–µ–љ вЖТ —Б–∞-` alternation). **(2)** `data/tokenizer/segmentation_roots.json` += `pron_sol` вАФ uncovered while running new —Б–Њ–ї eval cases: `analyse("—Б–Њ“У–∞–љ")` previously returned only verb-root ¬Ђ—Б–Њ“У–∞¬ї (Reflexive paradigm) parses, no ¬Ђ—Б–Њ–ї + Dat¬ї, because –±are —Б–Њ–ї wasn't in the lexicon at all (despite being a top-tier demonstrative pronoun). 1-line lexicon fix. **(3)** Eval test set extended +4 cases: bunda_anaphoric (–±“±–ї Loc), sogan_dative (—Б–Њ–ї Dat), magan_dative (–Љ–µ–љ Dat), sagan_dative (—Б–µ–љ Dat). **(4)** Frozen priors artifact regenerated вАФ closed-class boost now applies to 6 of 10 entries (was 5 at v4.20.5; —Б–Њ–ї newly included). **Results (n=23):** baseline 78.3 %; chain-only strategies 91.3 % (improved from 89.5 % at v4.21.0 вАФ chain priors handle most new cases without root help, because pronoun parses have higher chain prior scores than content-word alternatives); **chain_tiebreak_root 23/23 = 100.0 %**. All v4.21.0 –Њ–љ–і–∞ cases continue to resolve correctly + all 4 new v4.21.5 cases flip to their gold pronoun roots. Pipeline: paradigm table 6 вЖТ 21 + 4 unit tests + segmentation_roots += pron_sol + eval JSON +4 cases + artifact regen + printout version. Workspace tests **814 вЖТ 818 passing** (+4 pronoun_paradigm). Cadence: patch. **Stripe (4) вАФ compositional ML вАФ measurement layer remains CLOSED at 100 % under extended test set.** Next: v4.22.0+ (broader FST irregularity catalog вАФ irregular noun stems, possessive-stem alternations, voicing edge cases).

**v4.21.0 вАФ pronoun stem-alternation paradigm + 100 % accuracy on parse-disambiguation eval.** First minor in v4.21+ FST irregularity arc. v4.20.5's debug pass surfaced the actionable diagnosis: the FST returned no parse with root=`–Њ–ї` for ¬Ђ–Њ–љ–і–∞¬ї because Kazakh's phonological alternation `–Њ–ї вЖТ –Њ–љ-` (lateralization `–ї вЖТ –љ` before consonant-initial dental suffixes) wasn't modelled. v4.21.0 ships the irregularity as a small hardcoded paradigm matcher and **closes the entire v4.19.0вАУv4.20.5 measurement arc with `chain_tiebreak_root` reaching 100 % accuracy on the parse-disambiguation eval**. **(1)** New module `crates/adam-kernel-fst/src/pronoun_paradigm.rs` вАФ irregular-form table for Kazakh pronouns. v4.21.0 ships the `–Њ–ї` paradigm (–Њ–љ–і–∞ / –Њ–љ—Л / –Њ–љ—Л“£ / –Њ“У–∞–љ / –Њ–і–∞–љ / –Њ–љ—Л–Љ–µ–љ вАФ 6 oblique cases). **(2)** `try_pronoun_paradigm(surface, lex)` consulted by `analyse()` after the regular noun/verb passes вАФ strictly additive, no disturbance of existing candidates. The bare pronoun root is looked up via `lex.get(...)`; missing lexicon entry degrades silently. **Why hardcoded table not phonology rule:** general allomorph rules `–ї вЖТ –љ/“У/–і` would over-trigger on consonant-final nouns (–µ–ї вЖТ *–µ–љ-, –±–µ–ї вЖТ *–±–µ–љ-); linguistic reality is closed-class irregularity, exactly captured by listing the surface forms. **(3)** `pronoun_paradigm` exported from lib.rs for downstream extension. **(4)** Frozen priors artifact regenerated вАФ –Њ–љ–і–∞ tokens now produce 2 distinct roots, correctly classified as ambiguous and skipped from root counting; closed-class boost (√Ч10 from v4.20.5) keeps `P(–Њ–ї)=-3.24 > P(–Њ–љ)=-5.06`. **Results (n=19):** baseline 78.9 %; chain-only strategies 89.5 %; chain_plus_root 94.7 %; **chain_tiebreak_root 100.0 %** вАФ both –Њ–љ–і–∞ cases (sentence-initial + mid-sentence) now correctly resolve to –Њ–ї. **+21.1pp absolute lift over baseline.** This release closes a 6-release arc (v4.19.0 вЖТ v4.21.0) that surfaced and resolved the chain-collision blind spot. The combined system: chain priors handle regular cases; root priors + closed-class boost provide the chain-collision tiebreaker; FST stem-alternation makes closed-class oblique forms available as candidates. Each layer has clear responsibility, clear-typed artifact, transparent eval reporting. Pipeline: 1 new module + 5 unit tests + analyse() augmented + lib.rs exports + artifact regen + eval JSON RESOLVED notes. Workspace tests **809вЖТ814 passing** (+5 pronoun_paradigm). Cadence: minor. **Stripe (4) вАФ compositional ML вАФ measurement layer CLOSED at 100 %.** Next: v4.21.5 (extend paradigm with –±“±–ї / —Б–Њ–ї / –Љ–µ–љ / —Б–µ–љ / –Љ—Л–љ–∞—Г / –∞–љ–∞—Г + new eval cases), v4.22.0+ (broader FST irregularity catalog).

**v4.20.5 вАФ closed-class structural-pronoun boost + diagnostic discovery: –Њ–љ–і–∞'s gold parse isn't an FST candidate.** Patch in v4.20+ root-axis arc. Implements the closed-class boost planned by v4.20.0's writeup, then surfaces the **third (and most actionable) negative finding**: priors-side fixes were targeting the wrong layer the entire time. **(1) New** `data/lexicon/closed_class_root_boosts.json` вАФ hand-curated multiplicative count boosts for structural pronouns (–Њ–ї/–±“±–ї/—Б–Њ–ї/–Љ–µ–љ/—Б–µ–љ/–Њ–ї–∞—А/–±—Ц–Ј/—Б—Ц–Ј/–Њ—Б—Л/–Љ—Л–љ–∞—Г/–∞–љ–∞—Г). Compensates for v4.20.0's pronoun under-counting. **(2)** Training binary updated вАФ reads boost file (graceful fallback), applies multiplicative factor to `root_counts` AFTER unambiguous-only counting and BEFORE Laplace smoothing. **No schema bump** (still v4) вАФ boost folds into existing `root_log_prob`. **(3)** Eval binary `ADAM_DEBUG_TIEBREAK=1` env-gated debug pass dumps per-parse chain key, chain score, root score, picked parse. **Boost validation:** `–Њ–ї` flipped from -5.45 вЖТ **-3.24** (now above `–Њ–љ` at -5.06); `–±“±–ї`: -5.09 вЖТ -3.10; `—Б–µ–љ`: -6.96 вЖТ -5.44. 5 of 10 boosted roots applied (other 5 never appeared unambiguously). Boost mechanism works as designed. **THE CRITICAL FINDING:** eval results unchanged вАФ `chain_tiebreak_root` STILL picks `–Њ–љ` for both –Њ–љ–і–∞ cases. The debug logger reveals why: **the FST returns NO parse with `root=–Њ–ї` for ¬Ђ–Њ–љ–і–∞¬ї**. Both candidates have `root=–Њ–љ`. The gold parse isn't even a candidate. Reason: ¬Ђ–Њ–љ–і–∞¬ї starts with ¬Ђ–Њ–љ¬ї, not ¬Ђ–Њ–ї¬ї. The FST's prefix-match on root surface forms never considers ¬Ђ–Њ–ї¬ї (2 chars) for ¬Ђ–Њ–љ–і–∞¬ї (4 chars). Kazakh has phonological alternation `–Њ–ї вЖТ –Њ–љ-` before consonant-initial suffixes (locative `-–і–∞`, accusative `-–љ—Л`, dative `-“У–∞–љ`) вАФ regular lateralization. The lexicon has bare `–Њ–ї` as a pronoun root, but the FST has no machinery to generate the `–Њ–љ-` allomorph during analysis. **Implication:** three releases of priors-side architecture (v4.19.0/v4.19.5/v4.20.0/v4.20.5) were looking in the wrong layer. The priors infrastructure stays in place for genuine chain-collision cases вАФ but the –Њ–љ–і–∞ case can only be fixed at the FST/lexicon layer, not the scoring layer. This finding *unblocks* the project: eliminates an entire class of priors-tuning that would have continued to fail. Pipeline: 1 new data file + training binary boost-pass + eval debug logger + eval JSON notes updated. Workspace tests **809вЖТ809 passing**. Cadence: patch. **Stripe (4) вАФ compositional ML вАФ root axis layer continues, but next step pivots OFF priors.** Next: v4.20.10 / v4.21.0 (FST stem-alternation for pronoun paradigm вАФ add `–Њ–љ-`/`–Њ“У-`/`—Б–Њ“У–∞–љ-`/`–Љ–∞“У–∞–љ-` allomorphs so –Њ–љ–і–∞/–Њ“У–∞–љ/–Љ–∞“У–∞–љ/–±“±–љ–і–∞ surface the correct pronoun root as a candidate). Once the gold parse is *available*, v4.20.0's root prior + v4.20.5's closed-class boost will pick it under `chain_tiebreak_root` вАФ at which point –Њ–љ–і–∞ finally flips.

**v4.20.0 вАФ root-level priors + new prior axis (P(root) marginals via unambiguous-only attribution).** First minor in v4.20+ root-axis arc. v4.19.5 surfaced the structural finding that chain-level priors can't disambiguate root identity when both parses share a chain (–Њ–љ–і–∞: `–Њ–љ+Loc` and `–Њ–ї+Loc` collide). v4.20.0 builds the missing axis: a root-level marginal `P(root)` over the corpus, trained via **unambiguous-only attribution**, with two new evaluation strategies that combine it with the chain prior. **The empirical result is itself the second negative finding in a row** вАФ but the architectural foundation is in place, the failure mode is precisely diagnosed, and the next steps are sharp. **(1) Schema bump v3 вЖТ v4** вАФ new `SuffixPriors::root_log_prob` field; `load()` rejects v3. **(2) New constructor `from_counts_with_bigrams_and_roots`** вАФ third axis on top of v4.16/4.17 chain+bigram+POS. **(3) New method `score_root(root)`** вАФ log P(root) with Laplace smoothing and floor. Empty-priors path returns 0.0 (additive identity). **(4) Training binary updated** вАФ root counts via **unambiguous-only attribution**: token contributes to root only when `analyse()` returns parses with a single distinct root. Per v4.19.5 finding, uniform 1/N would dilute chain-collision pairs (–Њ–љ–і–∞ вЖТ 0.5 –Њ–љ + 0.5 –Њ–ї) вАФ exactly where tiebreaker is needed. **(5) Frozen artifact regenerated** at schema v4: 1112 chains, **9338 roots** from 3.3M unambiguous-token instances, 530K ambiguous skipped (~13.9% ambiguity rate). 1.5 MB JSON. **(6) Two new eval strategies:** `chain_plus_root` (additive log-prob), `chain_tiebreak_root` (strict tiebreaker). **Results (n=19):** baseline 78.9%; chain-only strategies 89.5%; **chain_plus_root REGRESSES to 84.2%** (high-frequency root ¬Ђ–љ–µ–ї—Ц–Ї¬ї overrides correct chain pick); **chain_tiebreak_root holds at 89.5%** (no regression but no lift on –Њ–љ–і–∞). **Why –Њ–љ–і–∞ still doesn't flip:** unambiguous-only attribution systematically under-counts pronouns. `–Њ–ї` appears mostly in inherently-ambiguous forms (–Њ–љ–і–∞, –Њ–љ—Л, –Њ“У–∞–љ) which get filtered; digit `–Њ–љ` appears in many unambiguous numeric contexts (dates, ages). Result: corpus marginal `P(–Њ–љ) > P(–Њ–ї)`, even though pronoun is far more common in real Kazakh. Fix paths: **closed-class boost** (v4.20.5 вАФ hand-curate –Њ–ї/–±“±–ї/—Б–Њ–ї/–Љ–µ–љ/—Б–µ–љ/–Њ–ї–∞—А/–±—Ц–Ј/—Б—Ц–Ј with explicit prior boost), **lexical co-occurrence** `P(root | surrounding tokens)` (v4.21.0+), or **dialog-layer anaphor resolution** (bigger lift). Pipeline: schema v3вЖТv4 + 1 new field + 1 new constructor + 1 new method + 2 unit tests + training binary updated + frozen artifact regenerated + 2 new eval strategies. Workspace tests **807вЖТ809 passing**. Cadence: minor. **Stripe (4) вАФ compositional ML вАФ root axis layer opens.** Next: v4.20.5 (closed-class structural-pronoun boost), v4.21.0+ (lexical co-occurrence if needed).

**v4.19.5 вАФ sentence-context strategy + structural finding on root-vs-chain disambiguation.** Patch in v4.19+ measurement arc. v4.19.0 surfaced one residual failure (¬Ђ–Њ–љ–і–∞¬ї вАФ gold = `–Њ–ї + Loc` anaphoric, all isolated-token strategies pick `–Њ–љ + Loc` "in ten") and tagged it as needing "FST sentence-context plumbing." v4.19.5 builds that strategy and measures whether it actually helps. **It does not.** Publishable negative result вАФ the structural reason gives a clearer architectural direction than blindly adding more context layers. **(1)** New `with_context` strategy as 6th tier in `eval_parse_disambiguation`: walks the full eval sentence left-to-right, greedily picking each token's parse under bigram-aware Jelinek-Mercer smoothed scoring (mirrors `parse_input_inner` in `adam-dialog`), tracks `prev_chain` across tokens, returns the root that won when target token reached. Pure inline impl in eval binary вАФ no new public API, no production code change. **(2)** New eval case `onda_anaphoric_mid_sentence` вАФ companion to `onda_must_not_be_ten_locative`. Same ambiguity, but –Њ–љ–і–∞ appears MID-SENTENCE (¬Ђ–Ь–µ–љ—Ц“£ –Ї—Ц—В–∞–±—Л–Љ –±–∞—А, –Њ–љ–і–∞ —Б—Г—А–µ—В—В–µ—А –Ї”©–њ.¬ї) вАФ distinguishes "context unavailable" from "context available but unhelpful." **Results (n=19):** baseline 15/19 = 78.9%; all 5 prior strategies including with_context **17/19 = 89.5%**. `with_context` matches isolated-token strategies вАФ **no additional lift**. Both –Њ–љ–і–∞ cases (sentence-initial AND mid-sentence) still pick –Њ–љ. **Why context plumbing doesn't help:** both `–Њ–љ + Locative` and `–Њ–ї + Locative` produce the SAME suffix chain (`noun:None|Singular|None|Locative|None`). Chain-level priors вАФ unigram, bigram, smoothed, POS-conditioned вАФ score these two analyses **identically**. Stable lex order picks –Њ–љ. The runtime layer doing context-aware re-ranking can't fix this; the signal needs to come from a different axis вАФ **root-level priors** `P(root | suffix_chain)`, lexical co-occurrence, or genuine anaphor resolution at the dialog layer. This reshapes v4.20+ direction: next compositional ML layer is about adding root-identity to the prior axis, not deeper context plumbing in the FST. Pipeline: 1 binary extension (~50 lines) + 1 new eval case + 1 updated note. No production code changes. Workspace tests **807вЖТ807 passing**. Cadence: patch. **Stripe (4) вАФ compositional ML вАФ measurement layer continues.** Next: v4.20.0+ (root-level priors to break the chain-collision tie), v4.20.5+ (corpus expansion + retraining).

**v4.19.0 вАФ empirical eval of v4.15+ priors.** First minor in the v4.19+ measurement arc, long-deferred from v4.17.5. v4.15.0 вЖТ v4.17.0 shipped four prior strategies (unigram вЖТ bigram вЖТ smoothed вЖТ POS-conditioned) with anecdotal REPL evidence but no measured accuracy. v4.19.0 closes that loop. **Architectural addition:** `data/eval/parse_disambiguation_eval.json` вАФ 20 hand-labeled cases of ambiguous Kazakh surface forms drawn from past live-REPL bugs (v3.9.5 –љ–µ–ї—Ц–Ї—В–µ–љ вЖТ –љ–µ–ї—Ц–Ї, v4.3.5 –Њ–љ–і–∞ вЖТ –Њ–љ, v4.4.10 “Ы—Л—Б“Ы–∞—Б—Л / –µ—И—В–µ“£–µ) plus cross-domain ambiguous content nouns (—В—Ц–ї, –Ї”©–Ј, —И–∞–є, –Ї“ѓ–є, —В–∞—Б, –±–∞—А, –Ї–µ–ї, —В–∞—Г, —И”©–ї, –µ–ї, –Ї“ѓ–љ, –Ї”©–њ, ”©–Ј, “Ы–∞–Ј–∞, –∞–ї–Љ–∞, –ґ–Њ“Ы). Each case: surface, sentence context (for human review), gold root, note explaining the ambiguity. **New binary** `eval_parse_disambiguation` in `adam-corpus`: loads eval set + Lexicon + trained `SuffixPriors`, runs `analyse()` per token, applies five scoring strategies (baseline lexicographic / unigram v4.15.5 / bigram v4.16.0 / smoothed v4.16.5 ќ±=0.3 / POS-conditioned v4.17.0), reports per-strategy accuracy + per-case detail (`=` / `вЪ†` markers). **Results (n=18 with non-empty FST parses):** baseline **15/18 = 83.3%**; all four prior strategies **17/18 = 94.4%** вАФ **+11.1 pp lift from priors over the lexicographic baseline**. The four prior strategies collapse to identical scores on isolated tokens (no preceding chain вЖТ bigram/smoothed/POS-conditioned all fall back to unigram) вАФ sanity check that higher-order tiers don't *regress* on no-context queries. Two cases where priors flip the wrong baseline pick: ¬Ђ–љ–µ–ї—Ц–Ї—В–µ–љ¬ї (baseline picks `–љ–µ–ї—Ц–Ї + Abl`, priors pick bare `–љ–µ–ї—Ц–Ї—В–µ–љ`) and ¬Ђ–∞–ї–Љ–∞¬ї (baseline picks verb `–∞–ї`, priors pick noun `–∞–ї–Љ–∞` = apple). One residual failure (all strategies): ¬Ђ–Њ–љ–і–∞¬ї вАФ gold = `–Њ–ї + Loc` (anaphoric "there"), priors pick `–Њ–љ + Loc` ("in ten") вАФ needs sentence context, beyond isolated-token scope. Two cases skipped (`“Ы–∞–Ј–∞`, `”©–Ј`) вАФ `analyse()` returns no parses; logged to stderr, removed from accuracy denominator. Pipeline: 1 new eval data file + 1 new binary + 1 `[[bin]]` registration. **No runtime code changes** вАФ pure infrastructure / measurement. Workspace tests **806вЖТ807 passing**. Cadence: minor. **Stripe (4) вАФ compositional ML вАФ measurement layer.** Next: v4.19.5+ (FST sentence-context plumbing for `–Њ–љ–і–∞`-class disambiguation), v4.20.0+ (corpus expansion + retraining priors over larger token base).

**v4.17.0 вАФ POS-conditioned priors P(chain | prev_pos, prev_chain) + 4-tier fallback ladder.** Third minor in the v4.15+ compositional-ML arc. v4.16.0 added bigrams, v4.16.5 added Jelinek-Mercer smoothing. v4.17.0 adds the **POS-aggregated fallback tier** вАФ when a full bigram row is sparse but the previous token's POS is known, fall back to the POS-conditioned distribution before dropping to the unigram. Adds robustness for sparse contexts without exploding the artifact size (POS axis = 2 dimensions). **Architectural addition:** new field `SuffixPriors::pos_transition_log_prob: HashMap<String, HashMap<String, f32>>` keyed by POS string (`"noun"` / `"verb"`) вЖТ curr_chain вЖТ log_prob. Schema bumped 2вЖТ3. **(1)** `from_counts_with_bigrams` extended to compute POS-aggregated rows in parallel with full bigrams (zero extra training cost вАФ same pass). **(2)** New helpers: `pos_from_chain_key(chain)` extracts POS prefix; `smooth_row(row)` extracted for code reuse. **(3)** Extended `score_chain_given_prev` 4-tier fallback ladder: **full bigram вЖТ POS-bigram вЖТ unigram вЖТ floor**. POS-bigram tier inserted when full-bigram row is empty OR sparse (curr unseen). Strictly additive: rich-context behaviour identical to v4.16.5. **(4)** SCHEMA_VERSION 2вЖТ3. **(5)** Training binary write_priors extracts `serialize_nested_map` helper used for both transition and POS-transition serialisation. **(6)** 1 new REPL replay regression dialog. **Frozen artifact regenerated** at schema v3: 1112 chains, 21270 full bigrams across 711 prev rows, **846 POS-bigrams across 2 dense rows** (noun: 423 successors, verb: 423 successors). 1.4 MB JSON (POS adds ~16 KB вАФ total artifact size effectively unchanged). Anti-regression 11/11 вАФ POS-bigrams only fire on sparse-bigram-row paths, which canonical queries don't walk. Pipeline: SuffixPriors +1 field, score_chain_given_prev +1 fallback tier, training binary refactored. Workspace tests **799вЖТ802 passing** (+3 unit tests). Cadence: minor. **Stripe (4) вАФ compositional ML вАФ fallback ladder layer.** Next: v4.17.5 (empirical eval вАФ tiny held-out test set of FST-ambiguous tokens with hand-labelled correct readings, measure how often v4.16.0/v4.16.5/v4.17.0 each pick the labelled parse vs raw v3.2.0 lexicographic).

**v4.16.5 вАФ Jelinek-Mercer interpolation knob ќ±¬Јlog_p_unigram + (1-ќ±)¬Јlog_p_bigram.** Patch in the v4.15+ compositional-ML arc. v4.16.0 shipped pure bigram scoring with three-tier fallback. v4.16.5 adds the **smoothing dial**: a tunable interpolation weight between unigram and bigram log-probabilities. Lets the runtime balance the bigram's specificity (good when context is rich) against the unigram's robustness (good when bigram rows are sparse). **(1)** New `SuffixPriors::score_chain_smoothed(curr, prev, alpha)` + `score_noun_smoothed` + `score_verb_smoothed` вАФ Jelinek-Mercer interpolation `ќ±¬Јlog P(curr) + (1-ќ±)¬Јlog P(curr|prev)`. `ќ±` clamped to [0,1]. Symmetric early-outs for `ќ±вЙИ0` and `ќ±вЙИ1` keep the hot path fast. **(2)** New `Conversation::with_priors_alpha(ќ±)` builder + `priors_alpha: Option<f32>` field. `None` preserves v4.16.0 pure-bigram-with-fallback path; `Some(ќ±)` switches re-ranker to interpolation mode. **(3)** `parse_input_with_priors` signature extended with `alpha: Option<f32>`; all 4 call sites updated. Older callers passing only `priors` get bit-identical behaviour. **(4)** `adam_chat` defaults to `ќ± = 0.3` (bigram-dominant with unigram smoothing). **Tunable via `ADAM_PRIORS_ALPHA` env var** for experimentation without recompilation. Startup line announces the chosen alpha. **(5)** 3 new unit tests (ќ±=0 = pure bigram, ќ±=1 = pure unigram, out-of-range clamps). **(6)** 1 new REPL replay regression dialog covers single-noun (minimal bigram) + multi-token (rich bigram) queries вАФ both must answer correctly under smoothing. **Why ќ±=0.3:** textbook Jelinek-Mercer for bigrams under Laplace-smoothed counts; bigram dominates (70%), unigram smooths sparse rows (30%). Empirically verified on 11-question anti-regression battery вАФ v4.16.0 behaviour preserved on every canonical query while making prior more robust to unseen contexts. Pipeline: SuffixPriors +3 methods, Conversation +1 field +1 builder, parse_input chain extended with alpha, adam_chat startup attaches ќ±=0.3 with env override. Workspace tests **796вЖТ799 passing** (+3 unit tests + 1 REPL replay). Cadence: patch. **Stripe (4) вАФ compositional ML вАФ smoothing patch.** Next: v4.17.0 (POS-conditioned priors `P(chain | prev_pos, prev_chain)` for sparse-mitigation).

**v4.16.0 вАФ context-aware priors P(chain | preceding_chain) + greedy bigram-aware FST parse selection.** Second minor in the v4.15+ compositional-ML arc. v4.15.0 shipped unigram priors `P(chain)`, v4.15.5 wired them into runtime parse selection. v4.16.0 extends to **context-aware bigrams** `P(chain | preceding_chain)` вАФ captures local morphological agreement (e.g. Genitive followed by 3sg-Possessive вАФ ¬Ђ–ґ–∞—Б—Г—И–∞–љ—Л“£ —П–і—А–Њ—Б—Л¬ї вАФ is much more probable than Genitive followed by Imperative). Same `–Ї–Њ—А–µ–љ—М + —Д—Г–љ–Ї—Ж–Є—П^n` compositional view, one Markov step deeper. **(1)** New `SuffixPriors::transition_log_prob: HashMap<String, HashMap<String, f32>>` field keyed by `(prev_chain, curr_chain)`. SCHEMA_VERSION bumped 1 вЖТ 2; v1 artifacts rejected by `load()`. **(2)** New `from_counts_with_bigrams` constructor with row-local add-one smoothing. **(3)** New `score_chain_given_prev` / `score_noun_given_prev` / `score_verb_given_prev` API with three-tier fallback ladder (no prev вЖТ unigram, unseen prev вЖТ unigram, unseen pair in known prev row вЖТ row floor). **(4)** Training binary updated with two-pass algorithm: first pass builds unique-token вЖТ chain-keys cache, second pass walks samples in order and tallies bigrams using the cache. Bigram pruning (count < 2.0) drops single-occurrence noise вАФ 305K observed pairs вЖТ 21K retained, ~6√Ч artifact size reduction. **(5)** Greedy bigram-aware parse selection in `parse_input_inner` вАФ tracks the previous token's selected chain key, passes it into `score_chain_given_prev` when re-ranking candidates. Sentence starts / FST-empty tokens reset context. Stable sort preserves v3.2.0 lexicographic order on equal-prior parses. **(6)** 1 new REPL replay regression dialog covers multi-token queries where bigram context matters. **Frozen artifact regenerated** as schema v2: 5,765,342 tokens, 1,112 chains, 305,856 bigrams observed вЖТ 21,270 retained, 711 transition rows; 1.4 MB JSON (was 70 KB unigram-only, well under 50 MB gitignore policy). 11-question anti-regression battery passes вАФ bigram-aware re-rank doesn't disturb any v4.x behaviour. Pipeline: SuffixPriors +1 field + 1 constructor + 3 API methods, SCHEMA_VERSION bump, training-binary upgrade, runtime integration. Workspace tests **793вЖТ796 passing** (+3 unit tests + 1 schema-version assertion bumped). Cadence: minor. **Stripe (4) вАФ compositional ML вАФ context-aware step.** Next: v4.16.5 (smoothing/interpolation knob ќ±¬Јlog_p_unigram + (1-ќ±)¬Јlog_p_bigram), v4.17.0 (POS-conditioned priors P(chain | prev_pos, prev_chain)).

**v4.15.5 вАФ SuffixPriors runtime integration: priors-aware FST parse selection.** Patch in the v4.15+ compositional-ML arc. v4.15.0 shipped the trained `SuffixPriors` artifact + `load`/`score` API but explicitly deferred runtime integration to keep the architectural addition reversible. v4.15.5 wires the prior into the parse pipeline as a re-ranking signal: each turn's FST candidate analyses are now sorted by `P(chain)` DESC before downstream consumers see them. **Strictly additive** вАФ when no priors are attached, the v3.2.0 deterministic lexicographic order is preserved bit-for-bit. **(1)** New `parse_input_with_priors` in lib.rs uses a stable comparator: parses scored higher by `P(chain)` move forward, ties retain the v3.2.0 lexicographic order. **(2)** `Conversation.suffix_priors: Option<SuffixPriors>` field + `with_suffix_priors(priors)` builder. **(3)** `Conversation::turn_with_trace` calls `parse_input_with_priors` with `self.suffix_priors.as_ref()`, threading the optional prior through the existing parse path. **(4)** `adam_chat` startup loads priors from `data/retrieval/suffix_chain_priors.json` (the v4.15.0 artifact), validates schema version, attaches via builder. Production startup now logs all four context layers: morpheme index, reasoning facts, domain index, **suffix priors (1112 chains over 5.77M training tokens)**. **(5)** Public exports tightened in adam-kernel-fst::lib. **(6)** 1 new REPL replay regression dialog locks v4.x baseline behaviour through the priors pipeline. Pipeline: 1 new lib function + new Conversation field + new builder + adam_chat startup integration.
